Trial Winning Decklists of Grand Prix Lyon 2018
===============================================



 Posted in **Event Coverage**
 on February 17, 2018 






![](https://media.magic.wizards.com/styles/auth_small/public/images/person/henke_author.jpg)
By Tobi Henke











The Grand Prix itself only started on Saturday morning, but the *Magic* action here in Lyon already began on Friday. Most importantly, the day's Trials offered players a final chance to earn byes for the weekend's main event, and a final chance to test their decks.


This being Modern, all kinds of decks passed the test, from Tron to Affinity, from Devoted Company to Devotion, from Burn to 8 Rack, from Humans to Elves to Merfolk. All of the lists below went undefeated through one of Friday's Trials, a first showcase of the vast variety of viable strategies we'd get to see over the course of the weekend.







#### Mehdi Guerroury's Moon Rat


##### 






![](https://web.archive.org/web/20160726232508im_/http://magic.wizards.com/sites/all/modules/features/wiz_bean_content_deck_list/icons/decklist_download.png)
